2416: অডিট লগ (SL-009) এ ট্যাক্স ক্যালকুলেশন ও ওভাররাইড ইভেন্ট রেকর্ড
2417: ডকুমেন্টেশনে ট্যাক্স রুল কনফিগারেশন প্রক্রিয়া বর্ণনা
2452: SL-001 – Canonical Posting / Journal Entry 
2454: 1. Overview (Developer Explanation)
2455: This SL implements the core journal entry and posting engine for OraBooks.
Critical guarantees:
2456: Central Posting Engine is the ONLY service that mutates ledger balances and creates ledger entries.
2457: AI never posts – AI provides only suggestions and confidence scores.
2458: Atomic transaction – All posting steps (ledger entries, balance updates, outbox) in a single DB transaction.
2459: Double-entry enforced at DB level – SUM(debit) = SUM(credit) per journal; unbalanced = HARD FAIL (never auto-suspense).
2460: Balance update uses normal_balance from accounts table (asset/debit normal: balance += debit-credit; liability/credit normal: balance += credit-debit).
2461: Idempotency unique constraint (org_id, idempotency_key) prevents duplicate posting.
2462: Outbox pattern – Events written within the same transaction; subledgers and read models updated asynchronously.
2463: Immutable hash chain – Canonical JSON serialization (sorted keys, UTC, fixed decimals) with previous_hash.
2464: Fiscal period validation – Blocks posting to closed periods (hard/soft close).
2465: Tenant isolation – All queries scoped by org_id.
2466: UTC timestamps everywhere.
2467: Approval segregation – Optional rule: creator cannot approve own journal.
2468: Fraud detection hooks – Events for rapid reversal, unusual amount, etc.
2469: Daily ledger integrity validator – Rechecks balances, hash chain, double-entry.
2470: 2. User View (What the user sees on screen)
2471: Journal list page:
2472: Table with journal number, date, type, total amount, status.
2473: Filters by status, date range, account.
2474: Journal detail page:
2475: Debit/credit lines (account code, amount, currency).
2476: AI confidence badge (e.g., “Confidence: 92% High”).
2477: Status badge (Draft, Review Pending, Approved, Posted, Locked, Reversed).
2478: Approve (green) and Reject (red) buttons – visible only to Approver/Owner.
2479: Post to Ledger button – visible only to Approver/Owner when status = Approved.
2480: Reverse Journal button – visible only to Owner/Admin when status = Posted/Locked.
2481: Tooltips:
2482: ✅ “Approving locks the journal. Posting is atomic.”
2483: 📌 “Posting updates ledger. Cannot be undone.”
2484: 🔄 “Requires a reason. Creates a reversing entry.”
2485: 🤖 “AI suggestion only. Human approves.”
2486: 3. User Journey (Step by step)
2487: User creates a transaction (invoice, expense, voice, CSV) → system creates a Draft journal.
2488: AI (optional) adds classification, confidence score, and risk evaluation.
2489: If confidence < 70% or risk > threshold, journal is sent to AI Review Queue (SL-076).
2490: Approver/Owner sees the journal in “Review Pending” state → clicks Approve or Reject.
2491: Reject → journal returns to Draft with a reason.
2492: Approve → status becomes Approved.
2493: Approver clicks Post to Ledger → triggers atomic posting.
2494: Posting succeeds → status becomes Posted and Locked (immutable).
2495: If an error is detected later, Owner/Admin clicks Reverse Journal → enters a reason → system creates a new reversal journal (as Draft) with opposite signs.
2496: Background workers: process outbox messages → update subledgers (AR, AP, Inventory, Tax), read models, and send notifications.
2497: 4. UI Components & Placement (Table)
2498: 5. Backend Actions (Step by Step)
2499: 5.1 Database Schema 
2500: sql
2501: -- ============================================================
2502: -- 1. ACCOUNTS (Chart of Accounts)
2503: -- ============================================================
2504: CREATE TABLE accounts (
2505:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2506:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2507:     code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
2508:     name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
2509:     type ENUM('asset','liability','equity','revenue','expense') NOT NULL,
2510:     normal_balance ENUM('debit','credit') NOT NULL,
2511:     system_generated BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
2512:     is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
2513:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
2514:     UNIQUE KEY uk_org_code (org_id, code),
2515:     FOREIGN KEY (org_id) REFERENCES organizations(id)
2516: );
2518: -- ============================================================
2519: -- 2. JOURNALS (Workflow)
2520: -- ============================================================
2521: CREATE TABLE journals (
2522:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2523:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2524:     journal_number VARCHAR(30) UNIQUE,              -- assigned only when posted
2525:     status ENUM('draft','review_pending','approved','posted','locked','reversed') NOT NULL,
2526:     transaction_date DATE NOT NULL,
2527:     idempotency_key VARCHAR(128) NOT NULL,          -- client-provided or generated
2528:     created_by INT NOT NULL,
2529:     approved_by INT NULL,
2530:     posted_by INT NULL,
2531:     approved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,
2532:     posted_at TIMESTAMP NULL DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2533:     reversal_of_id BIGINT NULL,
2534:     reversal_reason TEXT NULL,
2535:     source_type VARCHAR(50),                         -- 'invoice', 'expense', 'bank_feed', etc.
2536:     source_id BIGINT,
2537:     source_hash VARCHAR(64),                         -- hash of source document
2538:     journal_hash VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL,               -- SHA-256 of canonical representation
2539:     previous_hash VARCHAR(64) NULL,                  -- hash of last posted journal in org
2540:     metadata JSON,
2541:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
2542:     updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
2543:     UNIQUE KEY uk_org_idempotency (org_id, idempotency_key),
2544:     FOREIGN KEY (org_id) REFERENCES organizations(id),
2545:     INDEX idx_org_status (org_id, status),
2546:     INDEX idx_journal_number (journal_number)
2547: );
2549: -- ============================================================
2550: -- 3. JOURNAL LINES (corrected – no generated column with subquery)
2551: -- ============================================================
2552: CREATE TABLE journal_lines (
2553:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2554:     journal_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2555:     account_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2556:     account_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,              -- snapshot of account.code at line creation
2557:     debit_amount DECIMAL(20,2) DEFAULT 0,
2558:     credit_amount DECIMAL(20,2) DEFAULT 0,
2559:     currency_code CHAR(3) DEFAULT 'USD',
2560:     exchange_rate DECIMAL(12,6) DEFAULT 1,
2561:     base_currency_amount DECIMAL(20,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (debit_amount * exchange_rate) STORED, -- safe, no subquery
2562:     description TEXT,
2563:     FOREIGN KEY (journal_id) REFERENCES journals(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
2564:     FOREIGN KEY (account_id) REFERENCES accounts(id),
2565:     CHECK (debit_amount >= 0 AND credit_amount >= 0)
2566: );
2567: -- DB trigger for double-entry: AFTER INSERT/UPDATE, enforce SUM(debit) = SUM(credit) per journal.
2569: -- ============================================================
2570: -- 4. LEDGER ENTRIES (immutable posting record)
2571: -- ============================================================
2572: CREATE TABLE ledger_entries (
2573:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2574:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2575:     journal_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2576:     account_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2577:     debit_amount DECIMAL(20,2) DEFAULT 0,
2578:     credit_amount DECIMAL(20,2) DEFAULT 0,
2579:     posting_batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2580:     posted_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2581:     FOREIGN KEY (org_id) REFERENCES organizations(id),
2582:     INDEX idx_org_account_date (org_id, account_id, posted_at)
2583: ) PARTITION BY RANGE (YEAR(posted_at)) (
2584:     PARTITION p2024 VALUES LESS THAN (2025),
2585:     PARTITION p2025 VALUES LESS THAN (2026),
2586:     PARTITION p2026 VALUES LESS THAN (2027),
2587:     PARTITION p_future VALUES LESS THAN MAXVALUE
2588: );
2590: -- ============================================================
2591: -- 5. ACCOUNT BALANCES (current, normal_balance aware)
2592: -- ============================================================
2593: CREATE TABLE account_balances (
2594:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2595:     account_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2596:     balance DECIMAL(20,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
2597:     last_updated TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()) ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
2598:     PRIMARY KEY (org_id, account_id),
2599:     FOREIGN KEY (account_id) REFERENCES accounts(id)
2600: );
2602: -- ============================================================

2604: -- ============================================================

2606:     org_id INT NOT NULL,

2610:     PRIMARY KEY (org_id, snapshot_date, account_id)
2611: );
2613: -- ============================================================
2614: -- 7. POSTING BATCHES (sequential numbering per year)
2615: -- ============================================================
2616: CREATE TABLE posting_batches (
2617:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2618:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2619:     year INT NOT NULL,
2620:     batch_number INT NOT NULL,
2621:     started_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),

2623: );
2625: -- ============================================================
2626: -- 8. FISCAL PERIODS (hard/soft close governance)
2627: -- ============================================================
2628: CREATE TABLE fiscal_periods (
2629:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2630:     period_date DATE NOT NULL,
2631:     soft_closed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
2632:     hard_closed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
2633:     reopened_by INT NULL,
2634:     reopened_at TIMESTAMP NULL,
2635:     PRIMARY KEY (org_id, period_date)
2636: );
2638: -- ============================================================
2639: -- 9. OUTBOX MESSAGES (transactional outbox)
2640: -- ============================================================
2641: CREATE TABLE outbox_messages (
2642:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2643:     event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
2644:     aggregate_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2645:     payload JSON NOT NULL,
2646:     status ENUM('pending','sent') DEFAULT 'pending',
2647:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2648:     retry_count INT DEFAULT 0,
2649:     last_attempt TIMESTAMP NULL,
2650:     INDEX idx_status_created (status, created_at)
2651: );
2653: -- ============================================================
2654: -- 10. POSTING RETRY QUEUE (with manual review)
2655: -- ============================================================
2656: CREATE TABLE posting_retry_queue (
2657:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2658:     journal_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2659:     error_message TEXT,
2660:     retry_count INT DEFAULT 0,
2661:     status ENUM('pending','processing','failed','manual_review') DEFAULT 'pending',
2662:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2663:     FOREIGN KEY (journal_id) REFERENCES journals(id)
2664: );
2666: -- ============================================================
2667: -- 11. READ MODEL VERSIONS (tracking projections)
2668: -- ============================================================
2669: CREATE TABLE read_model_versions (
2670:     projection_name VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
2671:     version INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
2672:     rebuild_version INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
2673:     schema_version INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
2674:     last_updated TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP())
2675: );
2676: 5.2 Balance Update (Uses normal_balance)
2677: sql
2678: -- Stored procedure for correct balance update
2679: DELIMITER $$
2680: CREATE PROCEDURE update_account_balance(
2681:     IN p_org_id INT,
2682:     IN p_account_id BIGINT,
2683:     IN p_debit DECIMAL(20,2),
2684:     IN p_credit DECIMAL(20,2)
2685: )
2686: BEGIN
2687:     DECLARE v_normal_balance VARCHAR(6);
2688:     SELECT normal_balance INTO v_normal_balance FROM accounts WHERE id = p_account_id;
2689:     IF v_normal_balance = 'debit' THEN
2690:         UPDATE account_balances
2691:         SET balance = balance + (p_debit - p_credit)
2692:         WHERE org_id = p_org_id AND account_id = p_account_id;
2693:     ELSE
2694:         UPDATE account_balances
2695:         SET balance = balance + (p_credit - p_debit)
2696:         WHERE org_id = p_org_id AND account_id = p_account_id;
2697:     END IF;
2698: END$$
2699: DELIMITER ;
2700: 5.3 Atomic Posting (Pseudocode)
2701: python
2702: def post_journal(journal_id, user_id, idempotency_key):
2703:     with db.transaction():
2704:         # 1. Lock journal row
2705:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
2706:         if journal.status != 'approved':
2707:             raise ValidationError("Journal not approved")
2708:         if journal.created_by == user_id and config.CREATOR_CANNOT_APPROVE:
2709:             raise PermissionError("Creator cannot approve own journal")
2711:         # 2. Fiscal period validation
2712:         period = db.execute("SELECT * FROM fiscal_periods WHERE org_id = ? AND period_date = ?",
2713:                             journal.org_id, journal.transaction_date)
2714:         if period and period.hard_closed:
2715:             raise ValidationError("Fiscal period is closed")
2717:         # 3. Double-entry check (hard fail)
2718:         lines = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journal_lines WHERE journal_id = ?", journal_id)
2719:         total_debit = sum(l.debit_amount for l in lines)
2720:         total_credit = sum(l.credit_amount for l in lines)
2721:         if total_debit != total_credit:
2722:             raise ValidationError("Journal unbalanced. Cannot post.")
2724:         # 4. Assign sequential journal number
2725:         batch = get_next_posting_batch(journal.org_id, journal.transaction_date.year)
2726:         journal_number = f"JE-{batch.year}-{batch.batch_number:06d}"
2728:         # 5. Compute canonical hash (deterministic)
2729:         previous_hash = get_last_journal_hash(journal.org_id)
2730:         journal_hash = compute_canonical_hash(journal, lines, previous_hash)
2732:         # 6. Create ledger entries and update balances
2733:         for line in lines:
2734:             db.execute("""
2735:                 INSERT INTO ledger_entries (org_id, journal_id, account_id, debit_amount, credit_amount, posting_batch_id)
2736:                 VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
2737:             """, journal.org_id, journal.id, line.account_id, line.debit_amount, line.credit_amount, batch.id)
2738:             db.execute("CALL update_account_balance(?, ?, ?, ?)",
2739:                        journal.org_id, line.account_id, line.debit_amount, line.credit_amount)
2741:         # 7. Update journal record
2742:         db.execute("""
2743:             UPDATE journals
2744:             SET status='posted', posted_by=?, posted_at=UTC_TIMESTAMP(),
2745:                 journal_number=?, journal_hash=?, previous_hash=?
2746:             WHERE id=?
2747:         """, user_id, journal_number, journal_hash, previous_hash, journal_id)
2749:         # 8. Insert outbox message (async subledger & read model updates)
2750:         db.execute("""
2751:             INSERT INTO outbox_messages (event_type, aggregate_id, payload)
2752:             VALUES ('journal_posted', ?, ?)
2753:         """, journal.id, json.dumps({'journal_id': journal.id, 'org_id': journal.org_id}))
2755:         # 9. (Optional) fraud detection hook
2756:         if is_rapid_reversal_risk(journal):
2757:             db.execute("""
2758:                 INSERT INTO outbox_messages (event_type, aggregate_id, payload)
2759:                 VALUES ('fraud_risk_detected', ?, ?)
2760:             """, journal.id, json.dumps({'journal_id': journal.id, 'risk_type': 'rapid_reversal'}))
2762:     # Transaction commits here – background worker processes outbox
2763: 5.4 Canonical Hash Serialization (Deterministic)
2764: python
2765: def compute_canonical_hash(journal, lines, previous_hash):
2766:     # Sort lines by account_id for deterministic order
2767:     sorted_lines = sorted(lines, key=lambda l: l.account_id)
2768:     canonical = {
2769:         "org_id": journal.org_id,
2770:         "transaction_date": journal.transaction_date.isoformat(),
2771:         "lines": [
2772:             {
2773:                 "account_id": l.account_id,
2774:                 "account_code": l.account_code,   # snapshot
2775:                 "debit": str(Decimal(l.debit_amount).normalize()),
2776:                 "credit": str(Decimal(l.credit_amount).normalize())
2777:             }
2778:             for l in sorted_lines
2779:         ],
2780:         "previous_hash": previous_hash
2781:     }
2782:     # Sort keys, no extra spaces, separators compact
2783:     json_str = json.dumps(canonical, sort_keys=True, separators=(',', ':'))
2784:     return hashlib.sha256(json_str.encode()).hexdigest()
2785: 5.5 Idempotency & Retry Queue
2786: Idempotency: (org_id, idempotency_key) unique constraint in journals table. Client must provide a unique key for each post request.
2787: Retry queue: Only transient errors (e.g., DB lock timeout) go to posting_retry_queue with status pending. Background worker retries up to 3 times, then moves to manual_review. All other failures go directly to manual_review and trigger an alert.
2788: 5.6 Subledger Update via Outbox (Async)
2789: Background worker polls outbox_messages where status='pending'.
2790: For each journal_posted event, updates AR/AP/Inventory/Tax projections.
2791: On success, marks message as sent. On failure, increments retry_count; after max retries, moves to dead-letter table and alerts ops.
2792: 5.7 Anti-Corruption Layer for External Integrations
2793: python
2794: def map_external_transaction(source_type, raw_data):
2795:     # Convert Stripe, Shopify, CSV, etc. to canonical format
2796:     canonical = {
2797:         "source_type": source_type,
2798:         "source_id": raw_data.get("id"),
2799:         "source_hash": compute_hash(raw_data),
2800:         "transaction_date": parse_date(raw_data),
2801:         "lines": []
2802:     }
2803:     # ... mapping logic ...
2804:     return canonical
2805: # Then create journal from canonical data; never allow external raw writes.
2806: 5.8 Ledger Integrity Validator (Daily Job)
2807: python
2808: def validate_ledger_integrity(org_id, snapshot_date):
2809:     # 1. Recompute balances from ledger_entries since last snapshot
2810:     # 2. Compare with current account_balances
2811:     # 3. Verify hash chain: journal.previous_hash == previous journal's journal_hash
2812:     # 4. Check double-entry: for each journal, sum(debit)=sum(credit)
2813:     # 5. Report discrepancies to audit log and send alert
2814: 6. Dependencies (Other SLs that must be built first)
2815: Build order: SL-013 → SL-004 → SL-014 → SL-003 → SL-017 → SL-002 → SL-076 → SL-304 → SL-009 → SL-001
2816: 7. OraBooks Rules (Constitution References)
2817: Central Posting Engine (24.1) – Only this engine mutates ledger balances and creates ledger entries.
2818: AI never posts – AI only suggests; human must approve and post.
2819: Immutable ledger – No updates after posting; only reversal.
2820: Double-entry at rest – DB trigger ensures sum(debit)=sum(credit) per journal.
2821: Read/Write separation – Subledgers and reports updated asynchronously via outbox.
2822: Tenant isolation – All queries scoped by org_id.
2823: Atomicity – Entire posting in one DB transaction.
2824: Fiscal period lock – Closed periods reject posting.

├─ (reject) → Draft
├─ (if low confidence) → AI Review Queue
└─ (approve) → Approved

2891: SL-002 – AI Entry Approval Gate 
2892: This is the definitive, production-ready SL-002 specification. It includes explicit append-only protection for journal_approval_history, consistent status values (no rejected), and all enterprise governance features.
2893: 1. Overview (Developer Explanation)
2894: This SL implements the human approval workflow for journal entries.
Core guarantees:
2895: Only users with role approver or owner can approve/reject.
2896: AI never approves – AI only provides confidence scores (not stored in approval history).
2897: Every approval action is immutably logged in journal_approval_history.
2898: The history table is append-only: UPDATE and DELETE are prohibited at the database level (triggers or permissions).
2899: A snapshot hash of the journal content (lines, amounts, accounts, description, metadata excluding AI suggestions) is taken at submit and again at approval.
2900: revision_number counts content edits (increments on draft edits).
approval_round counts submit/resubmit cycles (increments when entering review_pending).
2901: Once approved, the journal is locked for editing. Editing an approved journal automatically invalidates approval (status returns to draft).
2902: Approval has a configurable expiry; posting (SL-001) checks approval_stale = false.
2903: Rejection does NOT use a separate rejected status. The journal remains draft, and a history record with action='reject' is created.
2904: Delegation, SLA escalation, MFA for high-risk approvals, and maker-checker policies are fully supported.
2905: All approval events publish outbox messages for notifications and read-model updates.
2906: 2. User View (What the user sees on screen)
2907: Pending Approval Queue – journals with status = 'review_pending', sortable by risk, amount, or age.
2908: Journal Detail Page (Approver/Owner only):
2909: Approve (green) – optional MFA for high amount.
2910: Reject (red) – opens modal requiring a reason.
2911: Resubmit – visible when status = draft and approval_round > 0.
2912: Edit – visible when status != approved.
2913: Approval History tab – table with action, performer, reason, snapshot hash, round, revision.
2914: Status badge – shows Draft, Review Pending, Approved, Posted, Locked, Reversed. A rejected journal shows Draft (backend) but UI may add (Rejected) hint from history.
2915: Tooltips:
2916: ✅ “Approve journal. Snapshot stored. Journal locked.”
2917: ❌ “Reject with reason. Journal returns to draft.”
2918: 🔄 “Resubmit after corrections. New approval round starts.”
2919: 🔒 “Approved journal is locked. Edit will invalidate approval.”
2920: 3. User Journey (Step by step)
2921: User creates journal (SL-001) → status = draft, revision_number = 1, approval_round = 0.
2922: Submit for Approval → status = review_pending, approval_round increments, snapshot hash computed, history submit recorded.
2923: Approver opens journal → reviews content.
2924: Approve → if amount ≥ threshold, MFA required. On success: status = approved, approved_snapshot_hash stored, expiry set, journal locked.
2925: Reject → reason required; status stays draft; history records reject. User can edit and resubmit.
2926: Edit (draft) → increments revision_number. If previously approved, invalidates (status→draft, history invalidate).
2927: Resubmit (from draft) → new approval_round, status = review_pending.
2928: Approval expiry – background job marks approval_stale = true after configured hours.
2929: Posting (SL-001) checks status = 'approved' and approval_stale = false before allowing ledger mutation.
2930: Delegation – Owner assigns delegate; delegate sees approval tasks.
2931: Escalation – overdue review_pending journals trigger reminders and secondary approver alerts.
2932: 4. UI Components & Placement (Table)
2933: 5. Backend Actions 
2934: 5.1 Database Schema (Final, Append-Only Enforced)
2935: sql
2936: -- ============================================================
2937: -- 1. Extend journals table (no 'rejected' status)
2938: -- ============================================================
2939: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN revision_number INT DEFAULT 1;
2940: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN approval_round INT DEFAULT 0;
2941: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN approved_snapshot_hash VARCHAR(64) NULL;
2942: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN approval_stale BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE;
2943: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN approval_expires_at TIMESTAMP NULL;
2944: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN lock_after_approval BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE;
2945: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN last_submitted_at TIMESTAMP NULL;
2946: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN last_submitted_by INT NULL;
2947: ALTER TABLE journals ADD COLUMN rejected_reason TEXT NULL;
2949: -- ============================================================
2950: -- 2. Append-only approval history (no UPDATE/DELETE)
2951: -- ============================================================
2952: CREATE TABLE journal_approval_history (
2953:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2954:     journal_id BIGINT NOT NULL,
2955:     action ENUM('submit','approve','reject','resubmit','delegate','escalate','invalidate','expire') NOT NULL,
2956:     performed_by INT NOT NULL,
2957:     reason TEXT NULL,
2958:     snapshot_hash VARCHAR(64) NULL,
2959:     approval_round INT NOT NULL,
2960:     revision_number INT NOT NULL,
2961:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2962:     FOREIGN KEY (journal_id) REFERENCES journals(id)
2963: );
2965: -- 🔒 Append-only enforcement (MySQL example)
2966: -- Option A: Application database user has only INSERT/SELECT privileges on this table.
2967: -- Option B: Triggers to block UPDATE/DELETE.
2968: DELIMITER $$
2969: CREATE TRIGGER prevent_history_update BEFORE UPDATE ON journal_approval_history
2970: FOR EACH ROW
2971: BEGIN
2972:     SIGNAL SQLSTATE '45000' SET MESSAGE_TEXT = 'UPDATE not allowed on approval history';
2973: END$$
2974: CREATE TRIGGER prevent_history_delete BEFORE DELETE ON journal_approval_history
2975: FOR EACH ROW
2976: BEGIN
2977:     SIGNAL SQLSTATE '45000' SET MESSAGE_TEXT = 'DELETE not allowed on approval history';
2978: END$$
2979: DELIMITER ;
2981: -- ============================================================
2982: -- 3. Delegation & Policies (same as before)
2983: -- ============================================================
2984: CREATE TABLE approval_delegations (
2985:     id BIGINT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
2986:     org_id INT NOT NULL,
2987:     delegator_user_id INT NOT NULL,
2988:     delegate_user_id INT NOT NULL,
2989:     starts_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
2990:     ends_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
2991:     created_by INT NOT NULL,
2992:     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT (UTC_TIMESTAMP()),
2993:     revoked_at TIMESTAMP NULL,
2994:     FOREIGN KEY (org_id) REFERENCES organizations(id)
2995: );
2997: CREATE TABLE approval_policies (
2998:     org_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
2999:     approval_expiry_hours INT DEFAULT 72,
3000:     reminder_hours_before_expiry INT DEFAULT 24,
3001:     max_approval_rounds INT DEFAULT 5,
3002:     maker_checker_required BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
3003:     mfa_amount_threshold DECIMAL(20,2) DEFAULT 10000.00,
3004:     escalation_after_hours INT DEFAULT 48,
3005:     escalation_role ENUM('admin','owner') DEFAULT 'admin'
3006: );
3007: 5.2 Core Functions (Pseudocode – Consistent)
3008: 5.2.1 Snapshot Hash (Canonical Scope)
3009: python
3010: def compute_journal_snapshot_hash(journal_id):
3011:     # Include: transaction_date, journal_lines (account_id, debit, credit, description, currency),
3012:     # source_type, source_id, metadata (excluding AI suggestions).
3013:     lines = db.execute("SELECT account_id, debit_amount, credit_amount, description, currency_code FROM journal_lines WHERE journal_id = ? ORDER BY id", journal_id)
3014:     data = {
3015:         "journal_id": journal_id,
3016:         "transaction_date": journal.transaction_date.isoformat(),
3017:         "lines": [{"account_id": l.account_id, "debit": str(l.debit_amount), "credit": str(l.credit_amount), "description": l.description, "currency": l.currency_code} for l in lines]
3018:     }
3019:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True, separators=(',',':'))).hexdigest()
3020: 5.2.2 Submit for Approval
3021: python
3022: def submit_journal(journal_id, user_id):
3023:     with db.transaction():
3024:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
3025:         if journal.status != 'draft':
3026:             raise ValidationError("Only draft journals can be submitted")
3027:         snapshot_hash = compute_journal_snapshot_hash(journal_id)
3028:         new_round = journal.approval_round + 1
3029:         db.execute("""
3030:             UPDATE journals SET status='review_pending', approval_round=?, last_submitted_at=UTC_TIMESTAMP(),
3031:             last_submitted_by=?, approval_stale=FALSE, approved_snapshot_hash=NULL,
3032:             approved_by=NULL, approved_at=NULL, rejected_reason=NULL WHERE id=?
3033:         """, new_round, user_id, journal_id)
3034:         db.execute("""
3035:             INSERT INTO journal_approval_history (journal_id, action, performed_by, snapshot_hash, approval_round, revision_number)
3036:             VALUES (?, 'submit', ?, ?, ?, ?)
3037:         """, journal_id, user_id, snapshot_hash, new_round, journal.revision_number)
3038:         insert_outbox('journal_submitted', journal_id, {'org_id': journal.org_id, 'round': new_round})
3039: 5.2.3 Approve Journal
3040: python
3041: def approve_journal(journal_id, user_id, mfa_verified=False):
3042:     with db.transaction():
3043:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
3044:         if journal.status != 'review_pending':
3045:             raise ValidationError("Journal not in review_pending")
3046:         policy = get_approval_policy(journal.org_id)
3047:         if policy.maker_checker_required and journal.created_by == user_id:
3048:             raise PermissionError("Creator cannot approve own journal")
3049:         total = get_journal_total(journal_id)
3050:         if total >= policy.mfa_amount_threshold and not mfa_verified:
3051:             raise MFARequiredError("High-value approval requires MFA")
3052:         current_hash = compute_journal_snapshot_hash(journal_id)
3053:         expires_at = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(hours=policy.approval_expiry_hours)
3054:         db.execute("""
3055:             UPDATE journals SET status='approved', approved_by=?, approved_at=UTC_TIMESTAMP(),
3056:             approved_snapshot_hash=?, approval_expires_at=?, lock_after_approval=TRUE
3057:             WHERE id=?
3058:         """, user_id, current_hash, expires_at, journal_id)
3059:         db.execute("""
3060:             INSERT INTO journal_approval_history (journal_id, action, performed_by, snapshot_hash, approval_round, revision_number)
3061:             VALUES (?, 'approve', ?, ?, ?, ?)
3062:         """, journal_id, user_id, current_hash, journal.approval_round, journal.revision_number)
3063:         insert_outbox('journal_approved', journal_id, {'org_id': journal.org_id})
3064: 5.2.4 Reject Journal (No separate 'rejected' status)
3065: python
3066: def reject_journal(journal_id, user_id, reason):
3067:     if not reason:
3068:         raise ValidationError("Rejection reason required")
3069:     with db.transaction():
3070:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
3071:         if journal.status != 'review_pending':
3072:             raise ValidationError("Journal not in review_pending")
3073:         db.execute("""
3074:             UPDATE journals SET status='draft', rejected_reason=?, approved_snapshot_hash=NULL,
3075:             lock_after_approval=FALSE, approval_stale=FALSE WHERE id=?
3076:         """, reason, journal_id)
3077:         db.execute("""
3078:             INSERT INTO journal_approval_history (journal_id, action, performed_by, reason, approval_round, revision_number)
3079:             VALUES (?, 'reject', ?, ?, ?, ?)
3080:         """, journal_id, user_id, reason, journal.approval_round, journal.revision_number)
3081:         insert_outbox('journal_rejected', journal_id, {'org_id': journal.org_id, 'reason': reason})
3082: 5.2.5 Resubmit After Rejection
3083: python
3084: def resubmit_journal(journal_id, user_id):
3085:     with db.transaction():
3086:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
3087:         if journal.status != 'draft':
3088:             raise ValidationError("Only draft journals can be resubmitted")
3089:         db.execute("UPDATE journals SET rejected_reason = NULL WHERE id = ?", journal_id)
3090:         return submit_journal(journal_id, user_id)  # reuse submit
3091: 5.2.6 Edit Journal (with invalidation)
3092: python
3093: def edit_journal(journal_id, user_id, new_data):
3094:     with db.transaction():
3095:         journal = db.execute("SELECT * FROM journals WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE", journal_id)
3096:         if journal.status == 'approved':
3097:             # Invalidate approval
3098:             db.execute("""
3099:                 UPDATE journals SET status='draft', approved_snapshot_hash=NULL, approved_by=NULL,
3100:                 approved_at=NULL, lock_after_approval=FALSE, approval_stale=TRUE,
3101:                 revision_number = revision_number + 1 WHERE id=?
3102:             """, journal_id)
3103:             db.execute("""
3104:                 INSERT INTO journal_approval_history (journal_id, action, performed_by, approval_round, revision_number)
3105:                 VALUES (?, 'invalidate', ?, ?, ?)
3106:             """, journal_id, user_id, journal.approval_round, journal.revision_number + 1)
3107:         else:
3108:             db.execute("UPDATE journals SET revision_number = revision_number + 1 WHERE id=?", journal_id)
3109:         # Apply the actual edits (update journal_lines, etc.)
3110: 5.2.7 Approval Expiry Background Job
3111: python
3112: def expire_stale_approvals():
3113:     rows = db.execute("""
3114:         SELECT id, org_id FROM journals
3115:         WHERE status='approved' AND approval_expires_at < UTC_TIMESTAMP() AND approval_stale=FALSE
3116:     """)
3117:     for jid, org_id in rows:
3118:         db.execute("UPDATE journals SET approval_stale=TRUE WHERE id=?", jid)
3119:         db.execute("""
3120:             INSERT INTO journal_approval_history (journal_id, action, performed_by, approval_round, revision_number)
3121:             VALUES (?, 'expire', 0, (SELECT approval_round FROM journals WHERE id=?), (SELECT revision_number FROM journals WHERE id=?))
3122:         """, jid, jid, jid)
3123:         insert_outbox('approval_expired', jid, {'org_id': org_id})
3124: 5.2.8 Posting Integration (SL-001)
3125: python
3126: def can_post(journal_id):
3127:     journal = db.execute("SELECT status, approval_stale FROM journals WHERE id=?", journal_id)
3128:     return journal.status == 'approved' and not journal.approval_stale
3129: 5.2.9 Delegation & Escalation (standard implementation, omitted for brevity)

3131: Rejection increments neither – only adds a history record.
